rgya gar skad du/ Ar+ya ta thA ga ta ma hA ka ru NA ni ra de sha nA ma ma hA yA na sU tra/ bod skad du/ 'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying rje chen po nges par bstan pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po dang po/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na bya rgod kyi phung po'i ri/ sngon rgyal ba bzhugs bzhugs pa'i mchod rten chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis brlabs pa sa'i snying po/ byang chub sems dpas mngon par bstod pa/ chos kyi gdan lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin gyis phyag byas pa'i sa phyogs/ dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par skul ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba chos kyi sgo mngon par brjod pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'byung ba/ yon tan tshad med pa las yang dag par byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul na/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid ni mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas/ chos kyi 'khor lo ni shin tu bskor/ slob ma shin tu dul ba mtha' yas pa'i tshogs ni mnga'/ chos thams cad la mnga' dbang ni brnyes/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa sgrub pa ni legs par mkhyen/ dbang po dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni brnyes/ sems can thams cad kyi bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba legs par 'joms pa la ni mkhas/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa lhun gyis grub pa ni rgyun mi 'chad cing dge slong stong phrag drug cu'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ thams cad kyang cang shes pa/ glang po chen po/ bya ba byas pa/ byed pa byas pa/ khur bor ba/ bdag gi don rjes su thob pa/ srid par kun tu sbyor ba yongs su zad pa/ yang dag pa'i shes pas sems shin tu rnam par grol ba/ shes rab shin tu rnam par grol ba/ nyon mongs pa'i bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba thams cad legs par bcom pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi rgyal po'i sras/ chos zab mo la gnas par mkhas pa/ dmigs pa med pa'i chos kyis nges par byung ba/ spyod lam mdzes pa phun sum tshogs pa/ sbyin pa'i gnas chen por gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' la shin tu zhugs pa sha stag go// byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun dpag tu med pa dang yang thabs cig ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad mkhyen pa chags pa med pa'i spyod yul gyis nges par byung ba/ byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po'i chos kyi sprin las lhag mthong dang / rig pa dang / rnam par grol ba'i glog phyung zhing bdud rtsi'i chu'i rgyun gyi char 'bebs pas 'gro ba thams cad tshim par byed pa/ sems can thams cad la sems sa dang mnyam pa rjes su chags pa dang / khong khro ba dang bral ba/ byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sna tshogs kyi lo thog yang dag par 'phel bar byed pa/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bas lhag pa'i shes rab kyi 'od zer rab tu gtong bas gti mug gi mun pa sel ba'i lam gyi snang ba thob pa kun tu ston pa dang / sems can gyi pad ma kha 'byed pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su smin par byed pa dang / sred pa'i chu skems pa dang / shes pa'i las kyi mtha' la rab tu 'jog pa la mngon par shes pa chen po dang / zhi gnas kyis rgyu ba/ zla ba lta bur 'gro ba thams cad la sems mnyam pas mngon par zhi bar bya ba'i bsam pa tshim par bya ba'i thabs la mkhas pas 'grib pa dang 'phel ba kun tu ston pa/ ri rab lta bu'i lhag pa'i bsam pas tshangs pa'i gnas pa'i rin po che shin tu brtan te/ ngos bzhi nas yul gyi rlung thams cad kyis mi sgul cing 'jig rten gyi chos las mngon par 'phags pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kun tu bstan pa snang bar gyur pa/ rgya mtsho chen po ltar gzungs dang dran pa'i snod rgya chen po chos kyi chus yongs su gang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rin po ches 'gro ba thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba/ kyi rgyal po ltar bden pa'i rkang pa dang / byams pa rab tu 'phel ba'i mjug ma dang / zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi mig dang ldan zhing chos zab mo la skrag pa med pas pha rol rgol ba thams cad 'joms pa/ bskal pa brgya stong phrag dpag tu med cing mtha' yas thug pa med par byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun ma bcad pas yon tan thams cad dang ldan pa sha stag dang thabs cig pa la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun nas snang zhing sgrib pa med par lta ba zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhing thams cad kyi rgyun bkod pa kun tu ston pa zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs las byung ba'i spyod pa'i blo gros zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyod lam thams cad kyis 'dul ba mi 'khrugs pa kun tu ston pa zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spobs pa mtha' yas pa'i tog gi rgyal mtshan rnam par sprul pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gser bzang po rnam par bsags pa'i 'od kyi gzi brjid kyi 'od zer zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyis rnam par nges pa'i tshig la spobs pa zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dpag tu med pas brtan pas bsags pa zhes bya ba dang / de la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po grangs med dpag tu med pa dag dang thabs cig go// de nas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'dug pas nges par 'byung ba sgrib pa med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs yang dag par rab tu ston to// de nas bcom ldan 'das mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas lo bcu drug bzhes te/ tshangs par spyod pa rgyas par gyur par mkhyen/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pa chen po de yang gzigs shing mkhyen te/ kye ma byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pa 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'dzin par mkhyen nas 'di snyam du gang gi phyir ngas byang chub sems dpa' rgya cher rjes su yongs su gzung ba dang / 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la gzud pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i cho 'phrul chen pos byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pas nges par 'byung ba sgrib pa med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs yang dag par bstan par bya'o snyam du dgongs so// de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas kyi yul rnam par sprul pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par ston pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin sangs rgyas kyi yul rnam par sprul pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par ston pa zhes bya ba de la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus steng gi bar snang la 'dod pa'i khams dang / gzugs kyi khams kyi bar du 'khor gyi khyams/ sangs rgyas kyi gnas de bzhin gshegs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas mngon par grub pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongs su sbyong ba/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams snang bar byed pa/ sems can tshad med pa'i bsam pa tshim par byed pa/ lha'i gzhal med khang thams cad zil gyis gnon pa/ phyogs bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par skul ba/ gzhi bai dUr+ya dkar po'i dbyibs dang / 'dzam bu'i gling gi gser gyi khang pa dag dang / dpal gyi snying po'i rta babs dag dang / rin po che rdo'i snying po'i sgo khang dag dang / nor bu rin po che snying po'i kha khyer dag dang / rin po che dri ma med pa'i 'od kyi stegs bu dag dang / rin po che kun nas 'od kyi khang pa brtsegs pa dag dang / rin po che thams cad kyis dgab pa dang / mu tig gi rgyan phreng rab tu spyangs pa dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan sgreng ba dang / lha'i dar gyi lda ldi mngon par spyangs pas bsngags pa bstan pa dpag tu med cing thug pa med pa stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad tsam zhig byung ste/ 'khor gyi khyams de yang tsan dan sbrul gyi snying pos bskus pa/ tsan dan dus kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i dri yid du 'ong ba dang ldan pa/ dri'i mchog a ga ru dam pa'i snying pos bdugs pa/ klu'i mu tig dang rin po che'i me tog gis rnam par spras pa/ me tog sil ma bkram pa/ rin po che'i shing dang / rin po che'i mkha' rten gyis mdzes par byas pa ste/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na rgyan mdzes pa bkod pa ji snyed pa de dag thams cad 'khor gyi khyams de nyid na kun tu snang ngo // der gdan seng ge'i khri bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag mang po dpag tu med pa/ grangs med pa/ sna tshogs pa/ blta na sdug pa/ mtho ba/ rab tu bzang ba/ yangs pa/ rgya che ba/ yid du 'ong ba/ yid dga' bar byed pa dag byung bar gyur to// gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir them skas kha khyer mi bdun gyi 'phang tsam gyis bskor ba/ rgyar dpag tshad phyed kyis yongs su bzung ba/ rin po che an da rnyil dang / mthon kha chen pos snying por gyur pa/ brgya byin thogs pa'i nor bu rin po che chen po'i gdugs can/ tshangs pa'i ne tso 'am ci dang / rin po che ser pos spras pa/ rin po che'i dril bu g.yer kha'i dra ba kun tu bskyod pas sgra 'byung ba/ sa'i steng nas 'khor gyi khyams la thug gi bar du gyen du mngon par 'phags pa/ drang ba ma yo ba bzhi stong byung bar gyur to// gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir ji lta ba bzhin du stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang de lta bu'i them skas chen po dag byung bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das dgongs shing mkhyen bzhin du ting nge 'dzin de las bzhengs par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das ting nge 'dzin de las bzhengs ma thag tu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rnam pa drug tu g.yos te/ snang ba chen po yang byung bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs dang thabs cig // nyan thos kyi tshogs dang thabs cig tu byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor cing nyan thos kyi tshogs kyis mdun du bdar te/ lha dang klus mngon par bstod cing me tog gi char chen po ni 'bebs/ na bza'i char chen pos ni mngon par 'gebs/ phye ma dang // spos dang / byug pa'i char chen po ni 'thor/ sil snyan dang / sgra dbyangs chen po ni rab tu sgrogs/ 'jig rten gyi khams dpag tu med pa ni rab tu g.yo bar mdzad/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa ni snang bar mdzad cing sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog tu gyur pa chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen pos bya rgod kyi phung po'i ri las mi snang bar gyur te/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po bye ba phrag du ma zhabs 'bring du 'brang zhing nor bu rin po che sna tshogs kyi them skas kyi dbus nas 'khor gyi khyams bkod pa ga la ba der gshegs so// de nas rgyal po chen po bzhi la sogs pa rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i me tog gi sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ nyi zla me dang nor bu'i 'od dang lha yul pa yi lha 'od shin tu dri med pa// thub pas 'od kyis thams cad zil gyis mnan nas ngan song gsum po dag kyang zhi bar mdzad// ri bo lhun po dang ni kho ra khor yug rtse mo bsnyil te zhing rnams gsal bar gyur pas na// dga' zhing yid rnams mgu nas don rnams thams cad grub pa'i rgyal ba la ni skyabs su mchi// de nas rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa'i zhabs 'bring du 'brang ngo // de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin la sogs pa sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i spos kyi sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ rdzu 'phrul dam pa brnyes shing rab tu mtshungs pa med pa rnam par 'phrul pa shin tu ston// rgyal ba nyi ma ji bzhin 'phags te zhing rnams bye ba brgya dag tu yang rab tu gda'// rgyal bas rang gi yon tan kun gyis zhing rnams thams cad brgyan te shin tu mdzes mdzad pa// gang zhig shin tu mnyam med mtshungs pa med cing rdzu 'phrul dbang du gyur la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'brang ngo // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab 'thab bral la sogs pa 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i na bza'i sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ bde gshegs khyod kyi mkhyen pa mtha' yas yangs pas sems can bsam pa mkhyen// mkha' 'dra'i lam gyi chos gsum dag la chags med thams cad mkhyen pa nyid// sems kyi 'jug pa gcig gis 'gro ba'i sems kyi spyod pa thams cad mkhyen// des na srid pa gsum po dag na lus can rnams kyis mchod par 'os// de nas 'thab bral gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'brang bar gyur to// de nas lha'i rgyal po rab dga' ldan la sogs pa dga' ldan gyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i rin po che'i sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ gang gi slad du sgra dang yi ge ma mchis gang du'ang rgyu ba ma mchis pas// khyod kyis chos rnams mi g.yo ya ma brla dang sgyu ma smig rgyu 'drar mkhyen nas// bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs rjes sems can rnams la ched du chos mchog gsungs pas na// chos kyi dngos po'i rang bzhin mkhas pa bdag med gsung ba'i rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'brang ngo // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab 'phrul dga' la sogs pa 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs par rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir lha'i rgyan gyi sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod do// chos kyi zong gis rang gi stobs bcu mkha' 'dra 'od zer ldan pa dang // thugs rje brnyes nas byams pa'i dgongs pas sems can rnams la gzugs ston pa// gru tshul chos la gnyis su med par zhugs kyang rgyal ba mtshungs par mkhyen// chos kyi khyad par sems lhag don kun grub pa'i rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'dis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'brang bar gyur to// de nas lha'i rgyal po dbang sgyur la sogs pa gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das them skas su zhugs pa dang / 'khor gyi khyams su mngon par phyogs par rig nas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las kyi phyir mu tig gi do shal gyi sprin gyi char rab tu phab ste/ thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod do// tshul khrims dri ma mi mnga' rnam dag rnam par nges pa dam pa ting nge 'dzin mchog mi g.yos pa// mnyam med blo ldan rgya mtsho 'dra bar gnas shing srid las rnam grol dbang sgyur zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// rim gyis byams dang ldan pa'i thugs rje yis ni bden pa'i lam gyi rnam pa rab tu gnas mdzad pa// rnam thar gsum gyi lam gyi khyams na gnas pa'i bde gshegs seng ge khyod la bdag cag phyag 'tshal lo// snying rje'i chu bo ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam 'phel ba// zhi gnas 'dab ma rnam par grol ba'i me tog rgyas// slob ma'i tshogs kyi bung bas nges par bsnyen gyur pa// bde gshegs pad ma la ni spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo// mnga' bdag g.yo ba ma mchis tshul khrims sar gnas pas// brtson 'grus mtshungs pa ma mchis stobs kyis yang dag 'phags// yul gyi rlung rnams langs pa chen pos mi g.yos pa// sangs rgyas ri bo dam pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// mnga' bdag thugs rjes dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor rnam dag pa// blo gter blo mchog gis ni rab tu 'joms mdzad pa// sems can brgya dag gis ni mang pos mchod gyur pa// bde gshegs zla ba khyod la bdag cag phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' ltar zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa'i lam gshegs pa// shes rab 'od kyis phyogs bcu dag ni rgyas 'gengs shing // skye bo mang po mtshungs med pad ma kha 'byed pa// sangs rgyas nyi ma dam pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// mnga' bdag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gsum po dag na yang // 'dren pa khyod dang mnyam pa dmigs par ma gyur te// khyod ni yon tan kun gyis yang dag grub pa lags// bdag cag khyod la bstod pas ngoms par 'gyur ma lags// lha dbang klu dang lha ma yin gyis phyag bgyis pa// lha mchog brgya dag gis kyang yang dag mngon bstod pa// bsngags pa brgya phrag mang pos yang dag mngon bstod pa// bde bar gshegs pa bstod 'os khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gis mngon par bstod nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs 'bring du 'brang ngo // de nas dang nyan thos chen po dag kyang stan ci rigs pa la 'khod par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin rnam par thar pa sgrib pa med pa la sangs rgyas rnam par rol pa gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa'i sems can rnams kyi sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba yang rgyun chad do// sems can thams cad kyang skad cig de la 'dod chags kyis gnod par ma gyur cing // zhe sdang gis ma yin/ gti mug gis ma yin te/ nyon mongs pa gzhan gyis kyang gnod par ma gyur to// de'i tshe sems can thams cad kyang byams pa'i sems dang / pha ma lta bu'i 'du shes su gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' yang dag brtson 'grus chen po'i stobs kyis bskal pa dag las phyir phyogs spangs// gang gis yon tan dag ni phyogs bcu rnams na mthu ldan rab brjod pa// shAkya thub pa'i 'od yangs 'gro ba thams cad snang bar bltas pa/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa/ bsam pa tshim par byed pa zhig byung bar gyur to/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' me tog dpal gyi snying po chos thams cad la dbang sgyur bas de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan seng ge'i khri chen po bskul bar bsngags pa mtha' yas zhes bya ba mngon par sprul nas dran pa dang ldan zhing shes bzhin du ting nge 'dzin de las langs te/ gus pa dang bcas shing zhe sa dang bcas par thal mo sbyar nas bcom ldan 'das la tshigs su bcad de gsol pa/ nyi ma'i 'od kyis 'gro ba'i dgos pa rab tu bgyid// lha dbang gzi brjid yon tan sum cu rtsa gsum dga'// tshangs pa'i dbyangs kyis tshangs pa'i 'jig rten rnam par mdzes// sangs rgyas mthu yi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa 'di// chos rnams mi g.yo nam mkha'i rang bzhin ya ma brla// sgyu ma smig rgyu lta bu chu yi zla 'dra zhing // rje med byed pa po dang tshor ba po med par// mkhyen nas mgon po 'dir ni rnam par sgrub pa ston// bkod pa'i sems kyi dbang 'gro sems ni gzugs can min// rnam sgrub thams cad sems kyi rang bzhin dbang du 'gro// bkod pa thams cad 'dir ni sgyu ma'i rang bzhin 'dra// rnam sgrub bdag gis ma mchis gang na'ang gnas ma mchis// gang gis sems rgyun ma mchis rang bzhin dag 'tshal ba// de la glo bur gnas pa'i nyon mongs ma mchis so// rtog dang kun rtog yongs su rtog las sems grol ba// de ni sgyu ma'i rnam par sprul pa sna tshogs ston// sa steng rdul tsam mngon par 'phags pa ma mchis kyang // sa steng nor bu rin chen sna tshogs kun tu bstan// gdan gang bzhugs nas sems can bye ba 'dul 'gyur ba// khyod kyi seng ge'i khri gdan rab mdzes bdag gis bgyis// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan mchog dang dar gyi phreng ba bsgreng // de ni gang du'ang 'gro ba ma mchis 'ong ma mchis// khyod kyis gang nas chos rnams 'du ba mkhyen nas kyang // sems can dam pa rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs ston// tshangs pa'i dbyangs ldan legs shing shin tu bsrungs pa'i gsung // 'jig rten sgron ma mdzad pa bsod nams gzi brjid mang // bdag la thugs brtse'i slad du 'dzegs te gdan la bzhugs// rga dang 'chi dang na ba gcod pa'i chos bshad gsol// khyod la bsnyen bkur bgyi dang chos ni mnyan slad du// rnam dag sems can 'di rnams phyogs bcu dag nas lhags// gang gi don du lhags pa'i don de stsal du gsol// seng ge'i khri la bzhugs te chos kyang bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' me tog dpal gyi snying po chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba'i lhag pa'i bsam pa mkhyen nas gdan seng ge'i khri de la bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das sgrib pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa brnyes nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pas nges par 'byung ba sgrib pa med pa'i sgo zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs byang chub sems dpa'i lam bkod pa la dmigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo thams cad dang / stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa yongs su sgrub pa dang / ye shes kyi 'byung gnas chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba'i gzungs kyi phyag rgya'i sgor 'jug pa/ so so yang dag par rig pa la rnam par gtan la dbab pa la gzhol ba'i sgor 'jug pa/ mngon par shes pa chen po'i ye shes la gzhol ba'i sgor 'jug pa/ phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor la mi skye ba'i chos ston pa/ theg pa thams cad theg pa gcig tu mnyam pa nyid du yang dag par 'du ba/ chos kyi dbyings tshul gcig cing ma 'dres pa la 'jug pa/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang dbang po la 'jug pa/ ston pa snying po dang ldan pa/ chos rnam par gdon mi za ba/ bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'joms par byed pa/ tshul bzhin gyi chos kyi tshul la gzhol bar 'jug pa/ nyon mongs pa dang lta bar gyur pa thams cad 'dul ba/ chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi rjes su 'jug pa/ thub pa med par yongs su bsngo ba la mkhas pa'i thabs dang ye shes ston pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes la 'jug pa/ chags pa med pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyi sgor 'jug pa/ chos thams cad ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par nges pa ston pa/ rtog pa med pa dang rnam par rtog pa med pa mnyam pa nyid du 'jug pa/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs thams cad bsags pa'i phyir rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab mo mnyam pa nyid rtogs par byed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs mnyam pa nyid kyi rgyan dang ldan pa/ dran pa dang / blo gros dang / rtogs pa dang / mos pa dang / shes rab zad mi shes pa mngon par sgrub pa/ nyan thos kyi theg pas 'dul ba'i phyir 'phags pa'i bden pa'i tshul la 'jug pa/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pas 'dul ba'i phyir lus dang / ngag dang / sems rab tu dben par shes pa/ theg pa chen pos 'dul ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sar dbang bskur ba rab tu thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan thams cad brjod pa'i phyir chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba'i tshul la 'jug pa 'di lta bu'i chos kyi rnam grangs yang dag par rab tu bstan pa dang / bsnyad pa dang / bshad pa dang / bklag pa dang / gzung ba dang / rnam par shes par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su bskang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par sprul pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / 'khor gyi the tshom thams cad gcad pa dang / bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad tshar gcad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa 'bar bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa chen po yongs su thob par bya ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das gdan seng ge'i khri de la bzhugs so// // bam po gnyis pa/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' rin chen srog shing zhes bya bas sangs rgyas kyi rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor sangs rgyas kyi rgyan gyis brgyan par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' sgra bsgrags stobs kyi rgyal pos pad+ma bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gyi lag pa rnams su me tog gi lda ldi dag dang / me tog gi skon bu rnams byin gyis brlabs te/ me tog gi lda ldi dang / me tog gi skon bu de dag gis bcom ldan 'das dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad la mngon par 'thor ro// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' blo mchog rgya mtshos dri bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gyi spu'i khung bu thams cad du tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i drir byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' 'od zer dra ba can gyis 'od bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor la lus kyi 'od mtha' yas par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' snying rje chen po sems pas mig mi 'dzums pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par phyogs shing mig mi 'dzums par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' blo mtha' yas dri med kyis chos la mchog tu dga' ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor chos don du gnyer zhing chos la dga' ba dang mos par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' spobs pa'i rgyan bkod pas rab tu zhi ba dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor sgrib pa lnga rnam par sel bar byin gyis brlabs so// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyal pos brjed pa med par spyod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor byang chub kyi sems dran zhing de bzhin gshegs pa la dmigs pa mi brjed par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun nas snang ba zhes bya bas zil gyis mi non pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor bdud dang / phyir rgol ba bcom par byin gyis brlabs so// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' bdud rab tu 'joms pas bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i bdud rab tu 'joms pas bdud kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'i ting nge 'dzin de la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na bdud bye ba phrag brgya ji snyed pa de dag thams cad dpung dang bcas/ g.yog 'khor dang bcas te myur ba myur bar thabs su rang rang gi bdud kyi gnas nas mi snang bar gyur te/ 'khor gyi khyams rin po che bkod par bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'khod nas/ de dag gis bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ lha'i mchod pa rnam pa brgya stong phrag du mas bcom ldan 'das la mchod nas gus pa dang bcas shing zhe sa dang bcas par thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btab nas/ bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gsol ba 'tshal na bcom ldan 'das chos bshad du gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa chos bshad du gsol/ byang chub sems dpa' bdud rab tu 'joms pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis bdag cag bdud kyi sug las 'dor zhing slan chad sems can rnams la mig gis mi rtsol bar 'gyur ba'i las mi bgyid do// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la dbugs dbyung ba stsol cig dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi thad du mchis te/ bdag cag chos nyan par bgyid do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bdud de dag dbugs dbyung ba'i phyir 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// grogs po dag legs so legs so// gang gi phyir khyed bdud kyi las kyang 'or la de bzhin gshegs pa la chos bshad par gsol ba yang thob shig dang / de nyid khyed kyi bdud kyi lam thams cad las 'da' ba'i rgyur 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sangs rgyas la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun pa'i stobs bskyed pa'i phyir ro// grogs po dag 'di lta ste/ dper na mun pa mun nag lo du mar bsags pa ni mar me gcig gis med par 'gyur ro// grogs po dag de bzhin du nyon mongs pa'i mun pa mun nag bskal pa brgyar bsags pa yang ye shes kyi stobs bskyed pa gcig gis med par 'gyur ro// grogs po dag 'di lta ste/ dper na zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gcig dang / nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gcig dang / nor bu rin po che chen po gcig gis mun pa mun nag thams cad sel to// grogs po dag de bzhin du dge ba'i sems lhag mthong dang ldan pa gcig gis mi shes pa'i mun pa mun nag thams cad sel to// grogs po dag de'i phyir khyed dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis rim gyis mi shes pa'i mun pa mun nag thams cad bsal nas chos kyi snang ba chen po thob par 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po zhes bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur te 'dug pa des bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi yul de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs pa dang / kun tu bstan pa 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo// deng ni de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pas nges par 'byung ba sgrib pa med pa'i sgo zhes bgyi ba 'dus pa chen po'i le'u'i chos kyi rnam grangs bshad par bzhed par the tshom ma mchis so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das e ma byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi 'dus pa 'di ni che ste/ bcom ldan 'das 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i go cha bgos pa/ mngon par shes pa'i ye shes chen pos rnam par rol pa/ phyogs bcur sgra bsgrags pa sems shin tu byang bar bgyis te dri ma ma mchis par rig pa dang / rnam par grol bas snang bar gyur pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bstod cing bsngags pa/ chos thams cad la dbang phyug gis dbang sgyur ba/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu son pa/ thabs la mkhas pa thams cad las nges par skyes pa/ bdud kyi las dang rtsod pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad bsal ba/ phas kyi rgol ba dang / ngan pa'i tshogs can gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu 'dul ba/ tshig thams cad rab tu dbye ba bstan pa shes pa la mkhas pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa chags pa ma mchis pa'i pha rol tu son pa/ dran pa dang / blo gros dang / rtogs pa dang / khrel yod pa dang / mos pa dang / gzungs dang / ye shes rab tu thob pa/ byin gyi rlabs thogs pa ma mchis shing spobs pa rgyun mi 'chad pa// sems can thams cad kyi dbang pos mchog dang / mchog ma lags pa shes pa la mkhas pa/ sems can thams cad kyi mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos ston pa/ 'khrul pa ma mchis par kha na ma tho ba ma mchis pa'i chos ston pa/ sems can thams cad kyi sgra dang skad la mkhas pa/ mi 'am ci dang / bya ka la ping ka dang / khrung khrung gi sgra dang / tshangs pa'i sgra dbyangs can/ shin tu bshes gnyen bgyis pas sems can thams cad yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa la 'god pa/ byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po'i lhag pa'i bsam pa can/ brtan zhing shin tu gnas la mi g.yo zhing ji skad smras pa de bzhin du bgyid pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng bar bgyid pa/ rdo rje ltar sra zhing mi shigs pa'i khor yug lta bu/ smon pa ma mchis pa'i smon lam dang ldan pa/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab mo blta dka' zhing rtogs par dka' ba la zhugs pa/ chad pa dang / rtag pa'i mtha' gnyi ga dang / lta bar gyur pa thams cad dang / bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba yang dag bcad pa/ tshogs can chen po'i tshogs kyi rgyal po yongs su 'gugs pa/ ded dpon chen po bskal pa grangs med par chos dkon mchog gis bsod nams yang dag par bsgrubs pa/ smad pa dang / bstod pa dang / bde ba dang / sdug bsngal las log pa/ dga' ba dang / dang ba dang / mchog tu dga' ba'i chos la sems zhugs pa/ chos dkon mchog gi 'od zer dang ldan pa/ shes rab kyis ba dang / 'dul ba'i cho ga 'tshal ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos dkon mchog thams cad kyi mdzod yang dag par 'dzin pa/ bsngags pa mtha' yas pa dang yang dag par ldan pa/ bsod nams tshad ma mchis pa bsags pa/ rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la nye bar gyur pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mu'i bskal par bsngags pa mthar mi phyin pa 'di lta bu rnams kyi 'dus pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das de la bdag 'di snyam du/ bcom ldan 'das ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pas nges par 'byung ba sgrib pa med pa'i sgo zhes bgyi ba 'dus pa chen po'i le'u'i chos kyi rnam grangs phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos la dbang bskur ba/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyu dang 'bras bu chud mi za ba/ nges pa'i sems can rnams la rkyen nye bar sgrub pa/ ma nges pa'i sems can rnams la snying rje chen po nye bar sgrub pa/ log pa nyid du nges pa'i sems can rnams lam la 'dzud pa/ theg pa gsum la mos pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas byung bar gyur na ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos 'di lta bu 'di dag 'jig rten du 'byung bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das skyes bu dam pa 'di dag gis 'khor gyi khyams 'dir sems bskyed pa gcig gis bkod pa gang byin gyis brlabs pa 'di ni nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bskal pa brgya phrag stong du yang ston pa'i rngo mi thogs so// bcom ldan 'das de la bdag 'di snyam bgyid de/ e ma ji tsam du gang rdzu 'phrul gyis rnam par sprul pa'i cho 'phrul 'di lta bu 'di mthong yang nyan thos kyi theg pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la re ba skyed pa'i sems can shes rab 'chal pa can de dag ni ngo mtshar che ba snyam bgyid do// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa nyid kyis nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad zil gyis non pa'i slad du'o// bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ dper na shes rab 'chal pa'i rang bzhin can gyi mi la la zhig nor bu rin po che bai dUr+ya bor nas nor bu mching bu la dmigs pa snyam du sems pa dang / bcom ldan 'das gang dag theg pa chen po bor nas nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la dmigs par bgyi ba snyam du sems pa'i sems can dag ni 'dra ba nyid du bdag la gda'o// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang dag lhag pa'i bsam pas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / skyed par 'gyur ba de dag thams cad ni ring por mi thogs par chos 'di lta bu dang ldan par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal pos bstan pa 'di bshad pa na/ lha dang mir bcas pa'i skye dgu'i 'khor de las srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag sum cus bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba 'dus pa'i le'u'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa'i 'dus pa chen po de gzigs nas/ e ma byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pa 'di dag ni chos don du gnyer ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'dzin par mkhyen nas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pas nges par 'byung ba/ sgrib pa med pa'i sgo'i le'u'i chos kyi rnam grangs rab tu bshad pa'i phyir/ mi 'jigs pas spobs pa zhes bya ba'i 'od zer skyes bu chen po'i mtshan spyi gtsug nas byung ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis 'od zer de phyung ma thag tu de nas thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs la lan bdun bskor ba byas te/ byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po'i lus la lan brgyar bskor ba byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po'i spyi gtsug tu mi snang bar gyur to// 'od des byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po la reg ma thag tu/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal pos thams cad dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyi 'od dang / seng ge'i khri dang / lus brgya 'gyur du zil gyis mnan nas lam me/ lhang nge / lhan ne'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal pos de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs rig nas stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig la gzar nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas bcom ldan 'das kyi dbu'i gtsug gi drang thad kyi steng gi bar snang la rin po che'i gzhag pa rnams la dran pa med cing yid la byed pa med pa dang / yang dag par spong ba rnams la skye ba med pa dang 'gag pa med par shes pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyis lus dang sems dben pa dang / dbang po rnams la dbang po yongs su shes pa dang / stobs rnams kyis bdud dang nyon mongs pa thams cad tshar gcod pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyis chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dang / lam rnams la 'ong ba med pa dang 'gro ba med par shes pa ste bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ shin tu zhi ba'i phyir zhi gnas shes pa dang / rab rib dang bral ba'i phyir lhag mthong shes pa dang / chos kyi phung po rjes su rtogs pa'i phyir phung po shes pa dang / nam mkha'i khams dang mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir khams shes pa dang / grong stong dang mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir skye mched shes pa dang / bdag med pa'i phyir rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mi 'khrugs pa'i phyir bden pa shes pa dang / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin rab tu rtogs pas chos thams cad nges par rtogs pa shes pa ste/ brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag ste/ dgu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sngon gyi mtha' dag pas 'das pa shes pa dang phyi ma'i mtha' dag pas ma 'ongs pa shes pa dang / bar gyi mtha' dag pas da ltar byung ba shes pa dang / rgyu chud mi za bas nges pa rnams shes pa dang / rkyen phye bar sgrub pas ma nges pa rnams shes pa dang / yongs su smin par byed pas log pa nyid du ma nges pa rnams shes pa dang / chos kyi skus rab tu phye ba'i phyir sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos kyi phyir chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa dang / 'dus ma byas kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir 'phags pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid du shes pa ste/ dgu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ rnam par bsgrub pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir sgyu ma lta bur shes pa dang / yongs su rtog pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir rmi lam lta bur shes pa dang / rnam par 'khrul pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir smig rgyu lta bur shes pa dang / 'pho ba med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi phyir gzugs brnyan lta bur shes pa dang / 'du 'phrod kyi mtshan nyid kyi phyir mig yor lta bur shes pa dang / rkyen gyi mtshan nyid kyi phyir brag ca lta bur shes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings 'dres pa med pa'i mtshan nyid du shes pa dang / de bzhin nyid gnas med pa'i mtshan nyid du shes pa dang / yang dag pa'i mtha' mi 'khrugs pa'i mtshan nyid du shes pa dang / 'dus byas dag 'dus ma byas kyi mtshan nyid du shes pa ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni gcig ste gcig gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dran pa brjed pa med pa ste/ 'di ni gcig go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni gnyis po 'di dag ste/ gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ kun tu 'dzin pa dang / 'dzin pa ste/ gnyis po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni gsum po 'di dag ste/ gsum gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ don la mkhas pa dang / tshig 'bru la mkhas pa dang / nges pa'i tshig la mkhas pa ste/ gsum po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bzhi po 'di dag ste/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chags pa med pa'i tshig dang / rtsub pa ma yin pa'i tshig dang / rab tu grol ba'i tshig dang / pa med pa'i tshig ste/ bzhi po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni lnga po 'di dag ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ thos pa thams cad kyi nang nas don la rton pa dang / yi ge'i tshogs thams cad kyi nang nas ye shes la rton pa dang / mdo sde thams cad kyi nang nas nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde la rton pa dang / gang zag gi sgra thams cad las chos nyid la rton pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad las 'jig rten las 'das pa la rton pa ste/ lnga po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni drug po 'di dag ste/ drug gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ ji skad smras pa de bzhin du byed pa dang / bden pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i tshig rab tu thob pa dang / nga rgyal med pas gzung bar 'os pa'i tshig dang / g.yo med pas blang bar 'os pa'i tshig dang / snying rje chen po la sbyor bas 'bras bu yod pa'i chos ston pa dang / snod la mkhas pas phyad par chos ston pa dang / 'jig rten shes pas dus su chos ston pa ste drug po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bdun po 'di dag ste/ bdun gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ mgyogs pa'i spobs pa dang / shugs can gyi spobs pa dang / myur ba'i spobs pa dang / chags pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / rgyun chad pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / 'khrul pa med pa'i spobs pa dang / shin tu nges pa'i tshig gi spobs pa ste/ bdun po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ lha'i skad shes pa dang / klu'i skad shes pa dang / gnod sbyin gyi skad shes pa dang / dri za'i skad shes pa dang / lha ma yin gyi skad shes pa dang / nam mkha' lding gi skad shes pa dang / mi 'am ci'i skad shes pa dang / lto 'phye chen po'i skad shes pa nas sems can thams cad kyi bar gyi skad shes pa ste/ brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni dgu po 'di dag ste/ dgu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'khor gyi nang du spa gong ba med pa dang / smra ba'i nang du zhum pa med pa dang / chos bshad pa'i nang du 'jigs pa med pa dang / 'dri ba rnams la nges par 'byung ba shes pa dang / mngon pa'i nga rgyal can rnams la snrel zhir bstan pa shes pa dang / yang dag par zhugs pa rnams la rjes su 'thun pa bstan pa shes pa dang / khengs pa dag la lag na rdo rje ston pa dang / mngon par chags pa rnams la sreg pa'i bskal pa ston pa dang / yongs su smin pa rnams la theg pa'i rim pa ji lta ba bzhin du ston pa ste/ dgu po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dogs pa thams cad la the tshom med par ston pa shes pa dang / blos chos skye ba'i sgo dang / shes rab kyi snang ba gzhan la lhag ma ma lus pa dang / yi ge bstan pa mi zad pa dang / don bstan pa rgyun chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bsngags pa mtha' yas pa yang dag par rab tu brjod pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa'i skyon mu med bar brjod pa dang / rnam par byang ba'i bsngags pa tshad med pa ston pa dang / dbang po thams cad la gzhol bar 'jug pa chags pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyis gnang ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa la 'jug pa shes pa ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gzungs kyi rgyan ni bcu po 'di dag go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don de nyid rgya cher bstan pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad ba 'di dag gsungs so// gang gis theg mchog dam pa 'di mdzes pa// blo gros chen po rnams kyi rgyan bzhi ste/ tshul khrims ting 'dzin de bzhin shes rab mchog // shin tu rnam nges don dang de bzhin gzungs// de ni lus can kun gyi yid 'od dga'// lus dang ngag rnams dang ni yid dag cing // de yi rnam par lhung ba kun chad pa// 'di ni tshul khrims ldan pa'i rgyan yin no// lha mi rnams kyi nang du mkhas pa skye// de yi smon lam ji ltar 'dod bzhin 'grub// nan tan snying por byed dang yang dag ldan// 'di ni tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan yin no// de yi ting 'dzin sgyu ma ma yin te// shes rab rnam grol de bzhin ye shes mthong // de yi mya ngan las 'das pa sgyu ma min// 'di ni tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims skyon med tshul khrims rnam par dag // tshul khrims sra sre ma yin 'dren ma med// de yi rang dga' de bzhin rang dbang yin// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// tshul khrims kyis ni sbyin pa dag par 'gyur// bzod pa dag cing de bzhin brtson 'grus dag // bsam gtan dag cing de bzhin shes rab dag // thabs dang de bzhin bag yod dag pa yin// g.yo ba med cing brtan la shin tu gnas// sa mchog thob cing rnal 'byor rnam 'phro med// lhod pa spangs shing dgang sla gso yang sla// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// brtson 'grus 'bar zhing tshul khrims bsngags pa ste// de yi sems ni nam yang gdung mi 'gyur// de la yid la gcags par 'gyur med de// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// 'jigs pa med cing mi skrag mi zhum ste// bsam pa des shing zhi la yid rab zhi// 'dir ni de yi bcings pa lhod par gyur// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// grags chen sems ni las su rung ba yin// de ni dul zhing de bzhin cang shes yid// 'dir ni rang lus mtshan gyis brgyan byed pa// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// de ni ji skad smras pa de bzhin byed// mkhas pa de ni ngag gi rgyan thob ste// de ni nyon mongs med pas rtag sems brgyan// 'di ni gang dag tshul khrims dag pa'i rgyan// khyad par 'phags pa'i zhing ni legs par brgyan// theg pa mchog la sems can yongs smin byed// gang phyir sdig pa thams cad mi byed pas// rang gi skye ba legs par brgyan par byed// byang chub spyod pa rtag tu brgyan byed cing // byang chub snying po dam pa brgyan par byed// stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dag brgyan byed cing // nga rgyal med pas shes pa legs par brgyan// de ni byams pas sems can kun khyab byed// mkhas pa rtag tu drang dang mnyen pa yin// g.yo ni med cing sgyu med bcos pa med// gti mug 'dod sdang 'jigs pas 'gro ma yin// de ni sgrib pa lnga po rnam par sel// bag yod gyur nas rjes su dran drug bsgom// byang chub yan lag bdun dang lam sgom ste// mthar gyis dgu dang ting 'dzin bsam gtan byed// rnal 'byor pa ni zhi gnas nges sems sbyor// de ni tshul bzhin dge ba chud mi gson// dben dang shin tu sbyangs dang so sor rtog // 'phags pa'i rigs la dbang ni sgyur ba yin// chos rnams la ni the tshom med par gyur// de la kun nas ldang dang 'gyod pa med// de la ma rig gti mug mun pa med// bden pa snang ba yongs su shes pa shes// tshul khrims dag pa dmigs pa med pa ste// shes rab dam pa bsam gtan ting 'dzin dag // gnyis bsal nas ni rnam par grol ba dag // lhag pa'i nga rgyal med cing shes pa dag // dus gsum dag la ye shes mthong mi chags// 'dod chags bral ba'i shes pas chos kyang dag // dag nas 'dir ni de la rlom sems med// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// shes rab kyis ni sbyin pa brgyan gyur te// rmi lam sgyu ma tshol ba med pa'i phyir// bdag dang byang chub de bzhin sems can rnams// 'khor gsum po dag de dag rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni tshul khrims brgyan gyur te// gzugs brnyan sgyu ma brag ca 'dra ba'i phyir// lus dang ngag rnams dang ni de bzhin sems// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni bzod pa brgyan gyur te// mkhas dang mtho min dma' bar 'gyur min dang // dam pa'i chos sku rtag tu rab rtog pa// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni brtson 'grus brgyan gyur te// skyo ba med cing bsam pa brtan pa dang // de ni blang ba med cing dor med pa// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni bsam gtan brgyan gyur te// de la ma chags gyur dang lhag mthong dang // mkhas dang mngon par shes pa skyed pa dang // 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam par sbyong // shes rab kyis ni thabs kyang brgyan byed de// shin tu sdud dang gzungs dang yang dag smon// 'khor gsum po dag de ni rnam sbyong zhing // sems can chos dang de bzhin zhing rnams sbyong // dran pa nye bar gzhag la dran mi 'jug // yang dag spong ba rnams la gnyis med de// rdzu 'phrul gyis ni lus dang sems kyang dben// sems can gyis ni dbang po kun mi shes// bdud dang nyon mongs rnams kyis zil mi non// chos kyi rang bzhin tshul bzhin rjes su rtogs// de bzhin lam la 'ong med 'gro ba med// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// de ni shin tu zhi bas zhi gnas shes// de yi lhag mthong spyod yul mtha' yas te// chos kyi phung po ci bzhin phung po shes// khams ni nam mkha' mtshungs shing 'dra bar shes// des ni stong pa lta bur skye mched shes// rten pas bsags pas chos rnams 'byung med de// don dam bden par 'khrugs pa med par shes// tshul bzhin gyis ni nges par rtogs par shes// dus gsum la ni chags med ye shes 'jug // rnam par gzhag phyir phung po gsum yang shes// dkon mchog gsum ni mtshan nyid gcig tu shes// 'di ni gang dag shes rab ldan pa'i rgyan// rnam bsgrubs mtshan nyid sgyu ma lta bur shes// yongs brtags rtsa ba rmi lam ji bzhin no// rnam 'phrul mtshan nyid smig rgyu 'dra ba ste// 'pho med chos rnams gzugs brnyan mtshan nyid do// 'du 'phrod byung ba mig yor lta bu ste// rkyen rnams kyis ni brag ca ji bzhin no// chos kyi dbyings ni rtag tu ma 'dres shes// de bzhin nyid ni gnas med de rab shes// yang dag mtha' ni rtag tu mi g.yo chos// 'dus ma byas dang 'dus byas gnyis su med// shes rab zab cing blo ni rab yangs par// brgyan nas sangs rgyas chos rnams tshol bar byed// de ni nam yang dran pa brjed pa med// chos rnams kun tu 'dzin cing 'dzin par byed// don dang tshig 'bru la ni rtag tu mkhas// nges tshig shes pa rtag par rtogs khong chud// chags med tshig dang rtsub pa ma yin dang // rab tu grol ba'i tshig dang med tshig // thos pa kun don rtag tu rtog pa dang // mkhas pa de ni ye shes rton par byed// nges don mdo sde rtogs par rab tu shes// gang zag med pa'i chos nyid rton byed cing // 'jig rten 'das pa'i chos nyid la yang rton// de ni gzungs kyis brgyan par gyur pa yin// de yi tshig ni bden pa'i rjes su 'thun// gzung bar 'os dang dus su 'os pa yin// de yi chos bstan de ni 'bras bu yod// phyed pa dang ni dus su rgyun chags 'jug // de yi spobs pa mgyogs pa skye ba ste// shugs can dang ni myur dang rtag mi chags// rgyun chad med dang 'khrul med nges pa'i tshig // legs par brgyus pa'i phreng bas legs brgyan bzhin// lha dang klu yi skad ni rab tu shes// gnod sbyin dag dang dri za lha min dang // mkha' lding mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye che// sems can kun gyi skad kyang rab tu shes// 'khor lhags shes nas spa gong med pa ste// smra ba mthong nas zhum par gyur pa'ang med// 'jigs pa med par chos kyi gtam yang rjod// 'dri ba rnams la nges 'byung rab tu shes// lhag pa'i nga rgyal can mthong snrel zhi yi// gtam brjod rnal 'byor mthong nas rjes su 'thun// nga rgyal can la lag na rdo rje ston// yul mngon chags la sreg pa'i bskal pa ste// theg pa gsum gyi rim pa'i gtam yang rjod// dogs pa kun gyi the tshom gcod pa ste// blo yi chos rnams mngon sum 'gyur ba yin// de yi shes rab nam yang gzhan mi ltos// yi ge thams cad rtag tu zad mi shes// don rnams nges pa dag la rgyun chags te// 'di ni sangs rgyas chos rnams mtha' yas brjod// de ni gzungs kyis brgyan par gyur pa yin// kun nas nyon mongs skyon ni mtha' yas shes// rnam par byang ba'i phan yon thug pa med// de bzhin sems can dbang po thams cad shes// sangs rgyas gnang ba'i so so rig pa thob// de ni gzungs kyis brgyan par gyur pa ste// de yi yon tan 'di dang gzhan dag kyang // bskal par rgyun chad med par rab brjod kyang // yon tan mtha' ni rtogs par mi nus so// // bam po gsum pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po la bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu snang ba gang dag gis snang bar gyur na byang chub sems dpa' mun pa mun nag dang bral zhing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa spyod par 'gyur ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dran pa'i snang ba dang / blo gros kyi snang ba dang / rtogs pa'i snang ba dang / chos kyi snang ba dang / shes pa'i snang ba dang / bden pa'i snang ba dang / mngon par shes pa'i snang ba dang / sgrub pa'i snang ba ste/ rigs sum tshogs par gyur pa dang / de dran pa phun sum tshogs par rig nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi grong khyer srung bar 'jog pa dang / dran pa sngon du 'gro bas chos thams cad la ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ don gyi blo gros yin gyi tshig 'bru'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / ye shes kyi blo gros yin gyi rnam par shes pa'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / chos kyi blo gros yin gyi nyon mongs pa'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / rig pa'i blo gros yin gyi 'gal ba'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / byang chub kyi sems kyi blo gros yin gyi nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi blo gros ma yin pa dang / rlabs po che'i blo gros yin gyi dman pa'i blo gros ma yin pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi blo gros yin gyi bdud kyi blo gros ma yin pa dang / snying rje chen po'i blo gros yin gyi sems can la rnam brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / dgongs te bstan pa rnams rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems can gyi bsam pa rnams rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i shes pa rnams rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab mo rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / snrel zhi'i rgyud bstan pa rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / spyi'u tshugs kyi rgyud bstan pa rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rtogs par khong du chud par 'gyur ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rtogs pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go / rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos kyi snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams la las kyi bya ba la 'jug pa ston pas 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / thar pa 'dod pa rnams la shes rab kyis ston pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / lam shin tu bsgoms pa'i phyir sgrib pa med pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / 'dod pa dang / srid pa dang / ma rig pa dang / lta ba'i zag pa mi slong ba'i phyir zag pa med pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / 'phags pa rnams kyi nges par gyur pa mngon sum du byed pa'i phyir 'dus ma byas pa'i chos kyi snang ba dang / glo bur gyi nyon mongs pa la shin tu rtogs dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ brgyad pa'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / rgyun du zhugs pa'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / dgra bcom pa'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi shes pa'i snang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i shes pa'i snang ba dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi mkhyen pa'i snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bden pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ bden pa bsgom pa gang gis nges par gyur pa la 'jug pa de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis 'bras bu dang po 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis 'bras bu gnyis pa 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis 'bras bu gsum pa 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis 'bras bu bzhi pa 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis rang sangs rgyas nyid 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis byang chub sems dpa'i bzod pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba dang / bden pa bsgom pa gang gis sangs rgyas kyi byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba de la de'i snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi bden pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go / rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag ste/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ lha'i mig gis gzugs thams cad yang dag par mthong ba'i phyir gsal ba'i snang ba dang / lha'i rna bas sgra thams cad thos pa'i phyir nges par rtogs pa'i snang ba dang / sngon gyi gnas bskal pa grangs med pa rjes su dran pa'i phyir rjes su dran pa'i snang ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems la lta ba'i phyir rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'i snang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing mtha' yas par rdzu 'phrul gyis 'gro ba'i phyir nam mkha' sgrib pa med pa'i snang ba dang / zag pa med pa'i shes pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir shes pa'i snang ba dang / sems can thams cad nye bar 'tsho ba'i phyir bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi snang ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi dogs pa gcod pa'i phyir ye shes kyi tshogs kyi snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa'i snang ba ni brgyad po 'di dag go// rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrub pa'i snang ba ni dgu po 'di dag ste/ dgu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sgrub pas ye shes kyi snang ba dang / sgrub pas shes rab kyi snang ba dang / sgrub pas blo'i snang ba dang / sgrub pas yang dag pa'i lta ba'i snang ba dang / sgrub pas zhi gnas kyi snang ba dang / sgrub pas lhag mthong gi snang ba dang / sgrub pas sems can gyi bsam pa'i snang ba dang / sgrub pas 'khrugs pa med par sems rnam par grol ba'i snang ba dang / sgrub pas shin tu mthar thug pa'i snang ba snang ba ste/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgrub pa'i snang ba ni dgu po 'di dag go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag gsungs so// dran pa de dang yang dag 'dres pa ni// sngon chad las dge bsags pa chud mi gzon// phra bar sngo ba phun sum tshogs pa de// phyi phyir zhing ni yang dag sgrub par byed// thos pa'i chos rnams la ni brjed pa med// rnam par nges pa myur du 'thob par 'gyur// nye bar zhi bas yul rnams las ni sbas// dran dang ldan pa mi dge rnams dang bral// dran pa rgya bo che ni shin tu bsags// bya ba bya ba dag ni rnam par 'byed// dran pa dag dang ldan par rig nas ni// rgyal ba rang byung dag gi byin gyis rlob// dam pa'i chos kyi grong khyer skyong byed pa// de ni 'gro ba rnams la chos ston nus// shes rab ldan pa mun pa rnam bral te// lha dang mi rnams kyi ni don kyang byed// blo gros bzang ldan snang ba thob gyur nas// dogs pa dang ni the tsom rnams kyang gcod// dran dang ldan pa rang 'byung ye shes kyis// byang chub myur du rjes su rtogs par byed// de ni don gyi blo gros can yin gyi// tshig 'bru'i rjes su mi rgyug sgra la'ang min// sems can dag pa ye shes blo gros can// rnam par shes pa'i blo gros 'dod ma yin// chos kyi blo gros ldan par gyur pa de// nyon mongs blo gros sel cing gti mug bral// shes rab dang ni thabs kyi tshul shes pa// de ni rgyal ba'i byang chub 'gal mi byed// de ni sangs rgyas 'gyur ba'i blo gros ldan// nyan thos 'gyur min rang rgyal 'gyur ma yin// rtag tu rlabs chen blo gros can yin gyi// de ni blo gros chung ngu 'dod ma yin// sangs rgyas blo gros rtag tu ldan yin gyi// bdud kyi blo gros su ni 'gyur ma yin// blo gros ldan pa snying rje cher gzhol gyi// sems can gang la'ang rnam par 'tshe ba min// chos 'ga' bstan pa gang yin de la ni// the tshom med cing rtogs par khong du chud// de ni dgongs te gsung la mkhas 'gyur zhing // sems can spyod pa rnams la rtogs dang ldan// so so yang dag rig la rtogs ldan zhing // de yi shes pa 'jug pa chags pa med// rkyen byung byed pa po dang rnam bral bar// rten pa'i chos rnams dag ni rab tu shes// de ni snrel zhi'i rgyu la mkhas gyur cing // spyi'u tshugs tshul ni rtogs par khong du chud// sangs rgyas kyi ni chos rnams ji snyed pa// thams cad kyang ni rtogs par khong du chud// 'jig rten pa yi chos kyi snang ba yis// lha mi rnams kyi las kyi bya ba shes// 'jig rten las ni 'das pa'i ye shes kyis// shes rab snang ba dang ni ldan pa yin// kha na ma thor bcas dang ma tho med// ye shes rab tu gsal ba chen po 'jug // lam ni shin tu bsgoms par gyur pa'i phyir// rtag tu 'bras bu yod par chos ston to// zag par bcas dang zag pa med pa yi// chos la de yi snang ba rab tu 'jug // de ni zag pa thams cad spong byed cing // lha dang mi rnams kyi ni don kyang byed// 'dus ma byas dang 'dus byas chos rnams la// de yi shes pa rtag tu rab tu 'jug // de ni de yis dri bral rab rib med// skyon med thob nas spyad pa rnams kyang spyod// rnam par byang dang kun nas nyon mongs la// de yi shes pa sgrib pa med pa 'jug // rang bzhin gyis ni sems 'od gsal ba dang // kun nas nyon mongs pa yi tshul yang shes// ji ltar mya ngan 'das par gyur pa ni// skye ba med cing 'byung ba med par shes// 'di 'dra 'di ni theg pa chen po la// chos kyi snang ba mtha' yas gyur pa yin// de ni brgyad pa yi ni shes pa dang // rgyun du zhugs la shes pa 'jug pa dang // lan cig phyir 'ong ba yi shes pa dang // phyir mi 'ong la shes pa 'jug pa dang // de ni dgra bcom pa dang rang rgyal dang // 'jig rten mgon po byang chub sems dpa' dag // kun la de yi shes dang sgrub pa rnams// lhag ma lus pa med par rab tu 'jug // gang gis 'bras bu 'thob par 'gyur ba dang // 'khrugs med don dam nges par 'byung 'gyur ba// de la rab bsgoms smra ba dpa' bo rnams// bden pa'i snang ba dag dang ldan pa yin// bden pa dag ni bsgom pa byas pas na// skyon med 'jug dang 'bras bu dang po 'thob// gnyis dang gsum dang de bzhin bzhi pa dang // rang rgyal rnams kyi 'bras bu thob par 'gyur// bsgom pa gang gis su ni smra ba'i stag // de dag bzod pa dag ni 'thob 'gyur dang // gang gis rgyal ba byang chub 'tshang rgya ba// bden pa de dag la ni snang bar 'gyur// lha yi mig gis su ni de yis kyang // gzugs kyi rnam pa dag ni thams cad mthong // lha yi rna ba nges par rtogs pa yis// phyogs bcu dag gi sgra rnams rtogs par 'gyur// sngon gyi gnas shes pa yi snang ba yis// bskal pa khrag khrig dag ni rjes su dran// 'od gsal ba yi shes pa'i snang ba yis// gzhan gyi sems kyi spyod pa rnams la mkhas// rdzu 'phrul gyi ni shes pa'i snang ba yis// phyogs bcu'i zhing ni khrag khrig rnams su 'gro// zag pa med pa'i shes pa'i snang ba ni// nam mkha' dang ni mtshungs shing 'dra ba yin// bsod nams kyi ni snang ba mtha' yas pa'i// mngon shes thog ma 'gro ba nye bar 'gro// de yi shes pa chags pa med pa yis// 'gro ba'i dogs pa dag ni gcod par byed// nan tan snying por byed pa'i rnal 'byor pa// dran dang blo gros rtogs dang chos shes snang // bden pa yi ni snang ba mtha' yas te// mngon par shes pa'i snang bar gyur pa yin// sgrub pas ye shes dang ni shes rab dang // rgya chen blo dang spobs pa mtha' yas dang // yang dag lta ba dang ni lhag mthong dang // shin tu 'khrugs pa med pa mthar thug gyur// snang ba shin tu rnam par dag pa brgyad// 'di dag mthu chen gang la yod pa ni// re zhig byang chub thob par ma gyur kyang // de ni sangs rgyas mdzad pa byed par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das kyis gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi dbang phyug gi rgyal po la bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu byang chub sems dpa' rnam pa bcu drug gis sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye'o// bcu drug gang zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du/ kye ma sems can 'di dag ni 'jig tshogs la lta bas bcings pa/ lta ba sna tshogs dang 'dres pa dag ste/ lta ba thams cad spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni yod pa ma yin pa'i phyin ci log tu gyur nas mi rtag pa la rtag par 'du shes/ sdug bsngal ba la bde bar 'du shes/ bdag med pa la bdag tu 'du shes/ mi sdug pa la sdug par 'du shes pa dag ste/ phyin ci log thams cad spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni ngar 'dzin pa dang / nga yir 'dzin pa la gnas pa/ dngos po med pa la dngos por 'du shes pa dag ste/ ngar 'dzin pa dang nga yir 'dzin pa spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni sgrib pa lngas bsgribs te 'dod pa'i zug rngus zug pa/ khong khro ba mang ba/ rmugs pa dang gnyid la chags pa/ dam pa ma yin pa la 'gyod pa kun nas langs pa/ zab mo'i chos la nges pa ma thob pa dag ste/ sgrib pa thams cad spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di ni skye mched drug gis chags pas chags te/ mig gis gzugs rnams mthong nas mtshan mar 'dzin cing mngon rtags su 'dzin pa yin/ rna bas sgra thos/ snas dri snams/ lces ro myangs/ lus kyis reg bya rnams la reg // yid kyis chos rnams rnam par shes nas mtshan mar 'dzin cing mngon rtags su 'dzin pa dag yin te/ skye mched drug gis chags pa spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni nga rgyal dang / lhag pa'i nga rgyal dang / nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal dang / nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang / mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang / snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang / log pa'i nga rgyal gyis bcom pas/ chung ngu dag pas bdag cag che'o snyam du bdag la rlom sems su byed pa/ mtshungs pa dag pas ni bdag cag che'o snyam du bdag la rlom sems su byed pa dang / ches che ba dag pas kyang bdag cag ches che'o snyam du bdag la rlom sems su byed pa/ gzugs la bdag tu khas len pa nas rnam par shes pa'i bar la bdag tu khas len pa/ ma thob par bdag la thob pa snyam du shes pa/ bdag cag ni 'phags pa'o snyam du bdag la sems pa/ log pa'i lta ba la yang dag pa'i lta bar mos pa dag ste/ nga rgyal gyi rnam pa thams cad spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni lam ngan par zhugs pa/ 'phags pa'i lam dang bral ba dag ste/ lam ngan pa spang zhing 'phags pa'i lam thob par bya ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni sred pa'i khol po chung ma dang / bu pho dang / bu mo la yongs su zhen pas sbags pa/ rang dbang med pas bdag la mi dpogs pa dag ste/ rang dbang yod cing bdag la dpogs par bya ba dang / gar dga' bar 'gro bar bya ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni phan tshun mi 'phrod pa/ khro ba dang / zhe sdang dang / gnod sems mang ba dag ste/ khro ba dang / zhe sdang dang / gnod sems spang bar bya ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni sdig pa'i grogs pos yongs su zin pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang bral ba/ sdig pa'i las byed pa dag ste/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa dang / sdig pa'i grogs po yongs su spang bar bya ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni brkam pa/ chags pas zil gyis non pa/ chog mi shes shing 'phags pa'i shes rab kyi gnas pa dang bral ba dag ste/ chags pa spangs pa dang / 'phags pa'i shes rab bskyed pa'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni las kyi rnam par smin pa med par lta zhing rtag pa dang chad pa la gnas pa dag ste/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab mo dang / las dang / bya ba la gzud pa'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni ma rig pa dang gti mug gis ldongs pa/ bdag dang / sems can dang / srog dang / gso ba dang / skyes bu dang / gang zag la mngon par zhen pa dag ste/ 'phags pa'i shes rab kyi mig rnam par dag par bya ba dang / lta bar gyur pa thams cad spang bar bya ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni 'khor ba la mngon par dga' ba/ phung po lnga'i gshed mas yongs su zin pa dag ste/ khams gsum thams cad las dbyung ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni bdud kyi zhags pa'i bcing bas bcings pa/ g.yo ba dang / rlom sems la gnas pa dag ste/ bdud kyi zhags pas bcings pa thams cad las rnam par dgrol ba dang / g.yo dang rlom sems spang ba'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba dang / kye ma sems can 'di dag ni mya ngan las 'da' ba'i sgo bcad cing // ngan 'gro'i sgo phye ba dag ste/ mya ngan las 'da' ba'i sgo dbye ba dang / ngan 'gro'i sgo bcad pa'i phyir de dag la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye ba ste/ rigs kyi bu rnam pa bcu drug po de dag gis sems can rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i snying rje chen po skye'o// rigs kyi bu 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi las ma 'dres pa sum cu rtsa gnyis te/ de dag la brtson na byang chub sems dpa' rnams legs par byed pa'i las byed pa rnams yin no// sum cu rtsa gnyis gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can dag gti mug gi gnyid kyis log pa dang / bdag shes rab kyis sad pa mthong nas shes rab kyis sems can rnams sad par byed pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i las ma 'dres pa dang po'o// sems can dag chung ngu la mos pa dang / bdag rgya chen po la mos par mthong nas theg pa chen po la sems can rnams yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag chos ma yin pa 'dod pa dang / bdag chos la gnas par mthong nas sems can rnams chos 'dod pa la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag 'tsho ba yongs su ma dag pa dang / bdag 'tsho ba yongs su dag par mthong nas sems can rnams 'tsho ba yongs su dag par sbyor ba dang / sems can dag lta bar gyur par bying ba dang / bdag yang dag pa'i lta bar zhugs par mthong nas sems can rnams 'phags pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag ma rig par gyur cing tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa bsags par mthong zhing bdag rig pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i tshul bzhin yid la byed pa la gnas par rig nas sems can rnams rig pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i tshul bzhin yid la byed pa la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag log pa'i chos la gnas pa dang / bdag yang dag pa'i chos la zhugs par mthong nas yang dag pa'i chos bsgrub par bya ba'i phyir sems can rnams la chos ston pa dang / sems can dag ser sna can du gyur te kun tu 'dzin pa'i sems dang ldan pa dang / bdag bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong bar mthong nas sems can rnams bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba la sbyor ba dang / sems can dag ngang tshul ngan pa can du gyur te/ sdom pa la mi gnas pa dang / bdag tshul khrims yongs su dag par gnas nas/ sems can rnams tshul khrims kyi sdom pa la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag gnod sems mang zhing khro ba shas che ba dang / bdag bzod pa'i stobs dang / byams pa la gnas par mthong nas sems can rnams bzod pa'i stobs dang / byams pa la gnas pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag le lo can du gyur te/ brtson 'grus chung ba dang / bdag le lo med cing brtson 'grus brtsams par mthong nas sems can rnams brtson 'grus rtsom pa la sbyor ba dang / sems can dag sems g.yengs shing dran pa nyams pa dang / bdag mnyam par bzhag ste/ bsam gtan la bsam gtan byed par mthong nas sems can rnams sems mi g.yeng ba dang / dran pa dang / shes bzhin la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag shes rab 'chal par gyur te/ dman zhing gti mug dang ldan pa dang / bdag shes rab dang ldan zhing gti mug dang bral bar mthong nas sems can rnams shes rab chen po dang / gti mug dang bral ba yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag rigs pa ma yin par lhung zhing ya nga ba'i byed pa brtsams pa dang / bdag thabs mkhas pa dang ldan zhing yang dag pa'i las brtsams par mthong nas sems can rnams thabs mkhas pa dang / yang dag pa'i las rtsom pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag nyon mongs pas bcom zhing kun tu rtog pa dang / rnam par rtog pa dang / yongs su rtog pa'i spyod yul par gyur pa dang / bdag nyon mongs pa thams cad las log par mthong nas sems can rnams nyon mongs pa thams cad spong ba la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i bcing bas bcings shing dmigs pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / bdag 'jig tshogs la lta ba yongs su shes pa dang ldan zhing dmigs pas bcings pa las yongs su grol bar mthong nas sems can rnams 'jig tshogs la lta ba yongs su shes pa dang dmigs pa dang bral ba la sbyor ba dang / sems can dag ma dul zhing ma sbas te byang ba ma yin pa dang / bdag dul zhing sbas te byang bar mthong nas sems can rnams dul ba dang / sbas pa dang / byang ba la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag byas pa mi gzo zhing byas pa mi shes te/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'joms pa dang / bdag byas pa gzo zhing byas pa shes te dge ba'i rtsa ba bsrung bar gnas par mthong nas sems can rnams byas pa gzo ba dang / byas pa shes pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba chud mi gzon pa la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag chu bor lhung zhing sdig pa 'dod pa'i dbang du song ba dang / bdag chu bo thams cad las yang dag par 'das par mthong nas sems can rnams chu bo thams cad las yang dag par 'da' ba la sbyor ba dang / sems can dag bka' blo mi bde zhing 'thun par 'dzin pa ma yin pa dang / bdag bka' blo bde zhing 'thun par 'dzin par mthong nas sems can rnams bka' blo bde zhing 'thun par 'dzin pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag phongs pa mang zhing dam pa ma yin pa la yongs su zhen pa dang / bdag ma phongs pa mang zhing dge ba bdud rtsi la gnas par mthong nas sems can rnams yongs su zhen pa dang bral zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba la gnas par sbyor ba dang / sems can dag dbul zhing 'phags pa'i nor dang bral ba dang / bdag 'phags pa'i nor dang ma bral zhing nor bdun dang ldan par mthong nas sems can rnams 'phags pa'i nor thob par bya ba la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag rtag tu na zhing khams rnam pa bzhi po'i sbrul gdug pas zin pa dang / bdag nad med cing bde la 'gyur ba med par mthong nas sems can rnams nad thams cad spong ba yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag mi shes pa'i mun pas kun tu gtibs shing ye shes kyi snang ba dang bral ba dang / bdag ye shes kyi snang ba thob par mthong nas sems can rnams ye shes kyi snang ba chen po la rab tu 'god pa dang / sems can dag khams gsum la chags pas chags shing rgyud lnga'i 'gro ba'i 'khor ba'i 'khor lo'i rjes su 'jug pa mthong zhing bdag khams gsum yongs su shes pa la mkhas par shes nas sems can rnams khams gsum yongs su shes pa la mkhas pa yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang / sems can dag g.yon phyogs kyi lam du zhugs shing g.yas phyogs kyi lam dang bral ba dang / bdag g.yas phyogs kyi lam ni 'di dag tu zad de/ 'di ltar phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched du btags pa'o// de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pas ji lta ba bzhin du mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// phyin ci ma log par mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// de dag ni sngon gyi ji lta bar phyis kyang de bzhin bar du yang de bzhin te/ sngon gyi mthar yang ma skyes/ phyi ma'i mthar yang mi 'pho/ bar du yang dben pa dag go// de ltar na 'di ni ji lta ba bzhin gyi gnas yin no// gcig ji lta bar thams cad kyang de bzhin/ thams cad ji lta bar gcig kyang de bzhin te/ ji lta ba bzhin la ni gcig pa'am mang bar mi dmigs so// ji lta ba bzhin gyi gnas 'di 'ang byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyis khong du ma chud pas de dag gis khong du chud par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rje chen po 'jug go// rigs kyi bu byang chub ni rnam pa la 'jug pas rnam pa med pa la zhugs pa'o// de la rnam pa ni gang // rnam pa med pa ni gang zhe na/ rnam pa zhes bya ba ni dge ba'i chos thams cad rtsom pa'o// rnam pa med pa zhes bya ba ni chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'o// rnam pa zhes bya ba ni gnas pa med pa'i sems kyi gnas so// rnam pa med pa zhes bya ba ni mtshan ma med pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rnam par thar pa'i sgo'o// rnam pa zhes bya ba ni chos rnams la sems pa dang / 'jal ba dang / bgrang ba dang / so sor rtog pa'o// rnam pa med pa zhes bya ba ni 'jal ba las shin tu 'das pa'o// 'jal ba las shin tu 'das pa gang zhe na/ gang la rnam par shes pa'i las med pa'o// rnam pa zhes bya ba ni 'dus byas la so sor rtog pa'o// rnam pa med pa zhes bya ba ni 'dus ma byas la mngon sum du byed pa'o// rnam pa dang rnam pa med pa la 'jug pa 'di yang byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyis khong du ma chud pas de dag gis khong du chud par bya'o snyam du sems can rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs rje chen po 'jug go// bdag rnam par dag pa gang yin pa dang / sems can thams cad rnam par dag pa gang yin pa de gnyis su med cing gnyis su dbyer med do// gnyis su med pa'i don gang yin pa de skye ba med do// skye ba dang 'gag pa med pas sems dang / yid dang / rnam par shes pa rnams mi 'jug go// gang la sems dang / yid dang / rnam par shes pa mi 'jug pa de la yongs su rtog pa gang gis tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed par 'gyur ba'i yongs su rtog pa gang yang med do// der tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang ldan pas ma rig pa kun nas mi slong ngo // gang ma rig pa kun nas mi ldang ba de srid pa'i yan lag bcu gnyis kun mi mthong ba de ltar mthong ngo // de la ci yang zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ mtshan ma dang dmigs pa'o// des gang gi tshe sems med pa dang dmigs pa med par mthong ba de'i tshe yang dag pa gros zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu de ltar na nam mkha' ji lta bar byang chub kyang de bzhin no// byang chub ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin no// chos rnams ji lta bar sems can rnams kyang de bas spyod pa'i bdag nyid mkhyen// de bzhin rna ba sna dang lce dang de bzhin lus// yid dang chos kyi khams kyang rtag tu stong par mkhyen// chu dang me dang sa dang rlung gi khams 'di dag // nam mkha' mnyam par mi yi seng ges rab tu mkhyen// 'dod pa dang ni gzugs dang gzugs med khams 'di dag // yongs su rtog las yang dag byung bar ma lus mkhyen// nyon mongs khams ni rgyal bas rang bzhin med par mkhyen// rnam byang rang bzhin 'dra bar bde bar gshegs pas mkhyen// mi mkhas dag gis 'khor ba rtag tu 'dus byas dang // mya ngan 'das pa gang la mtshan nyid gsum med dang // khams gang mi dge bas ni 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid dang // gang yang dge bas 'jug pa thams cad gcod pa dang // sna tshogs khams dang du ma'i khams can 'jig rten 'di// sangs rgyas mkhyen kyang ngas mkhyen snyam du rlom sems med// nam mkha' ji lta bzhin du mtha' yas phyogs rnams kyi// khams rnams de bzhin mi yi seng ges rab tu mkhyen// rgyal ba'i ye shes dam pa de ni thug pa med// de yi mtha' ni 'gro ba rnams kyis shes mi nus// 'di ni skyob pa rdul med rnams kyi 'phrin las bzhi// de yis sems can 'dul ba'i khams rnams cho ga mkhyen// gang dag las legs byas pas dul gyur de dag la// 'khrul pa brgya lam na yang nam yang mi 'byung ngo // rigs kyi bu gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pas sems can gzhan dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi dbang po'i rim pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen to// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pas ji ltar sems can gzhan dag dang / gang zag gzhan rnams kyi dbang po'i rim pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu mkhyen ce na/ rigs kyi bu 'di la de bzhin gshegs pas sems can dbang po khyad par du 'phags pa yang rab tu mkhyen to// dbang po dman pa yang rab tu mkhyen to// yongs su rtog pa'i dbang po ji lta bus mthar phyin pa'i 'dod chags skye ba dang / mthar phyin pa'i zhe sdang
